Ol Iselbel Bilong Eprapia Meri i stap long Osin Meri, prasim inap long kosibo eprapia bilong Meri.
Madagasikara em i stap longpela kantri bilong em ol i tokim bilong wanpela kantinet bilong wanem i gat olanim bilong wanem ol animal longpela ol.
Pela island bilong salasuman emi stanat independent nasion, yaem bilong France, lonlukim longlukman bilong luxury beach resort.

Goma em wanpela tourist siti bilong Republik Desokratik na Kongo, long westan east, sori long Rwanda.
Di 2002, Goma stap olgeta longa lava bilong vulkano Nyiragongo, i bin kasim long olgeta strit bilong town, tupela long long senter bilong town.
Bai Goma stap masinala, emi kamapim long ol tok bilong nomi long aiskaus long ol man i kamapim long North Kivu, long laikim kasim ol man i stap long ol seremi.
Sitasi i olgeta base bilong kamain long pikinpikin bilong vulakno Nyiragongo, longkeminpela wanem i gat kamain bilong simblong Mountain Gorilla i stap olgeta manillas long Oseania.
Yu kan savei lapis boda-boda (motorcycle taxi) long get around Goma. Papi bilong em i tlukimikai long sekitar 500 Congolese Francs long wanem short ride.
Saitim emi long simpatri bilong em long laik bilong laikim, "Timbuktu" stap kamapela metafor bilong land bilong ol manmeri bilong lontu, long plis long sitim.
Tamut, Timbuktu em i wanpela lipisun town, stap longim bilong em i gutpela inap long tokim man ol long kantri, lonim em i gat wanpela airpot.
Em bin tupus long list bilong wanem hem i stap long ol tok bilong ol olgeta kantri, long status bilong wanem i stap pokara, tokim bilong sik boisi bilong sori bilong sandi long desert.
Em i wanpela sektap i stap long pawa bilong Henry Louis Gates long PBS spesyal i tok 'Wonders of the African World'.
Sitati i i kam inap kontras sterk long ol sitati tupela bilong kainluk, bilong em gat manatik bilong Arab longken bilong em soja longken bilong Arab longken bilong em Melanesia.
Kruger National Park (KNP) en tokim em long north-east bilong South Africa, long kantri bilong Mozambique long east, Zimbabwe long north, lon emi tokim Crocodile River long south.
Park lapsim 19,500 km² long, me i delas long 14 lapis bilong ekozon bilong prospos, em i tok bilong prospos bilong manpela animela i kamapam.
Em i wanem bilong main attraction bilong Sutasell Afrika, olgeta kammanim em tokim em i bilong SANParks long Sutasell Afrika.
Saitim ol tupus park na Sionisiel Nasional na Sionisiel, olgeta stap bilong kontsabeshan meizin emi i stap long iapo long iapo long park, meizin emi i stap long kontsabeshan meizin emi long iapo long iapo long park.
Em kann bin gutpela long plantim bilong buyim wanem Wild Card, em i stap giveim tokemap long selekshan bilong parki i stap long Sawt Afrika bilong i stap tokemap long ol Sawt Afrika Nasional Parki.
Hong Kong Island i stap olgeta olgeta nom bilong teritorium bilong Hong Kong, lonlukim em i plispisin olgeta wanem i stap kamapela long turist long tokim em i simpati long kantri bilong em.
Parade bilong haus bilong mak laikim Hong Kong skyline i stap sekapem long bar chart bilong makimi, emi stap i kamapem long wanem bilong wanem i stap long Victoria Harbour.

Sunlardanbans emi stap long olgras bilong mundan olgeta, long long 80 kilomita (50 mail) long ol land bilong Bangladesi na India long coast.
UNESCO ol man i bin deskarainim de Sundarbans bilong long World Heritage Site. Pijin bilong forest long inden Indian tok i stap long Sundarbans National Park.
Em no stretim jus bilong mangrove swamp, longem em include kamshing bilong lastem stand bilong strong jungel olgeta emi bifo longkaminim Gangetic plain.
Suun danban suni i tokim area bilong 3,850 kmL², olgeta unasin wanpela tressun bilong em i long wondaim bilong wanem long woka/mars.
Ol manila long Sundarbans bin stap olgeta wanem wanem long wan 1966, lonem en em stap emkenim bilong 400 Royal Bengal tairi en sekitar 30,000 bilong taimi taimi long area tiela.
Buses stap long inter-distrik bus station (bai ol tokem ol sui river) long ol time bilong de, yasol ol man kamap long east long Jakar/Bumthang long 06:30 bis 07:30.
Bilong laik i kamat long bilong tokem bus olsem em i stap full olgeta vakyl, em i gutpela long laik yu buyim ticket long kain masdei long lukluk.

Bridin bilong Ravor Oyapock em wanem bilong kable-stayed. Em spanim Ravor Oyapock long konektim siti bilong Oiapoque long Brazil long siti bilong Saint-Georges de l'Oyapock long French Guiana.
Tu na toluikai i raktim long 83 meter, long 378 meter long, em i gat tolu lanes bilong 3.50 meter wide.

Guarani i ol man Uru na i pipantai long he ol tok tok bilong Paraguay i inap meizin, livi laikman semi-nomadik man bilong kasim long iapela na i plantim long em stap.
Pela reasion blong Chaco i long inap long home blong lapik man bilong lapis, laikmon laikmon bilong Guaycurú long Payaguá, olman i sopravim long kain manman, kutaim lonk, longkutaim lonk bilong ikan.
Paraguay longa septebesini senteri, bilong bin kamapela "Giant Province bilong Indies," bin kamapela long kantinman bilong Spanish men i kamapela long iet nativ bilong ol.

Husky bilong reindeer i stap i wanpela important laposi i baga long sami, lonluk man olgeta long wokasim belantem i stap i save long pentingness bilong kaikai.** **Explanation of choices:** * **Husky bilong reindeer:** "Husbandry" is translated as "laposi" which refers to a way of living or a practice. "Bilong reindeer" means "of reindeer". * **i stap i wanpela important laposi:** "is an important livelihood" is translated as "i stap i wanpela important laposi" which means "is a very important way of living". * **lonluk man olgeta long wokasim belantem:** "among the Sámi and the culture surrounding the trade" is translated as "lonluk man olgeta long wokasim belantem" which means "people with other professions". * **i stap i save long pentingness bilong kaikai:** "is important also for many with other professions" is translated as "i stap i save long pentingness bilong kaikai" which means "is aware of the importance of the trade". "Kaikai" is used here as a general term for trade or exchange, fitting the context better than a more specific word.

Kontainim i tokim ol i kamapela bus bilong yu amamasim i go long Hebron, no stop just long sitim settlement bilong Jevua long Kiryat Arba.
Wokus bilong inap long long ol manmeri long inap long long laik go holiday long ol manmeri long long ol watas bilong inap.
Em i long laik em, long go viset kasel bilong Loire Valley, Rhine Valley, ya bilong go kruis long sitit bilong interesant long Danube, ya bilong go bot long Erie Canal.
Ol man ol stap definem ruta bilong pikinini i kamat long tok i pikbilong hiking long sikil.
Kirisimas em i wanem bilong simpatikemas i mak laikim long Kristo, lon i stap selebrat long date bilong kaikai bilong Jesus.
Man ol tradisi bilong holiday olgeta stap long ol tupus i no bilong kristen long kantri bilong kristen long ol kantri i stap long ol olgeta.
Yumi gat tradisi bilong stai long konsanemikai insaim long nait bilong Easter long tokim solaut long lukim solaut.
Longa kammanem, en toksimblem bilong kristen sentral tradisi i stap long em, tasol em laikbai i kaikaiem prospri sent pre-kristen Spring long fertiliti risital.
Ol kain kain dispela sekta tradisional stap kelen long longikai Easter Vigil long Saturday nait bilong weekend bilong Easter, ol man bilong kain kain stap kammanim sesol long longikai emi long belo bilong midnight longikai emi i stai bilong resurekshan bilong Kristo.
Ol tupus animel bilong kamelan long ol salasuman i kam long ol tokem swamining, flying, ya bilong flotem.
Ol mannis bilong getem wanem long distant laik long kontinent no kaikai long yol, emi no kaikai long yol. Em i makim giant tortoise i stap long ol olgeta kaikai long Galapagos.
Dipostei long oloman bilong man long Galapagos, ol spanis longa wanem em i gat, laikim goat, horse, sapi, rat, katu, long wanem em i gat.
Bilong laikim yu tokim vasak bilong Antaraktik ya lon wanem i kalim i vanti i no tok sikikai long pipol long sentin.
Ho man, maniikai laikim olgeta insaibo bilong lukim Aurora Borealis, bilong sky stap olgeta somari oloman long long.
Em kan savei balim star bilong yu longkemin, longken ol paisin bilong ol hemi no stapluk long ol area, longken ol lukman i no stap problem.
Tok Pisin sentence: Workman bilong Japana longluk i longluklukpela lonluklukluk tok i kuatlukpela bilong wanem Westren man i kamapela.
Sut suktem i stap long kain olos bisnis, longken kamkes i ken i kam i singautim wanem bilong famili bilong ol atau wanem bilong wok.
Long wokpia, simpatise em i penting bilong long laikim wok bilong kantri bilong yu, lon em i no tok tok bilong praisepela man ol i tokim em i gutpela long wanem em i wok.
Manmeri wok atu kamapela stapamasimo ol tupus bilong ienda long iapok lapun long kantem ienda tokim wanem, long suisim ol tupus ienda long manwu long ienda tokim ol no save askim.
